[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical file path traversal issue was detected in the Apache Commons Compress [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“Expander” example code when exercised by a Jazzer-based fuzzer. The sanitizer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception after [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencountering a malicious input that used “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” sequences to break out of the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Issue Observed**  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing, the `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` harness invoked [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand` with a crafted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive input. The input contained path segments like [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m,” which resolved to a location outside the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesignated extraction directory. The Jazzer sanitizer for file path traversal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected this and threw a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Vulnerability Type**  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m traversal: an attacker-supplied path includes “..” segments[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto escape the target directory, potentially enabling overwriting or creation of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles outside the intended extraction root.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Key Observations and Findings**  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` → `checkPath` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`pathFirstArgHook`.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace highlights repeated calls to various `Expander.expand` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverloads [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating that the vulnerability can be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered in multiple expansion scenarios.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is only an entry point and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot the root cause; it feeds arbitrary byte sequences to the Expander logic.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer effectively blocks the unsafe write, but its intervention signals[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma gap in the Expander’s own validation or sanitization of archive entry paths.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Areas to Investigate**  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Expander.expand methods**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – All overloads of `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially at lines [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferenced in the trace: [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – How entry names from the archive are concatenated with the output directory.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Any pre-existing checks or normalization steps on entry paths.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Path resolution logic**  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The code that resolves `File` or `Path` objects for each archive entry.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Calls to `File#[0m[1;35mgetCanonicalPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or equivalent methods intended to prevent[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Integration with sanitizer hooks**  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The registration point where `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook` is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplied.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Whether sanitizer usage aligns with expected library behavior or if explicit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks should be baked into the Expander code itself.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Archive entry processing**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – How nested directories and symlinks within archives are handled.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – The mechanism for creating parent directories before writing files.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInvestigating these components will provide a holistic view of how path traversal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis currently mitigated and where the Expander implementation might require stricter[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput validation or path normalization.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFile path traversal: [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/expander-tmp9553408917715085303/output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:                final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m91[0m[39m:            nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m92[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m93[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis and Root Cause  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `Expander` class delegates path concatenation to [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The current `resolveIn` implementation first performs [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and checks that the normalized path stays [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin `parentPath`. However, it then URL-decodes `name` and calls [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without re-normalization or re-validating the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprefix.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A malicious archive entry name containing URL-encoded “..” segments [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bypasses the initial check when decoded, leading [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto a path outside the target directory.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Support for decoding entry names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto handle archives with URL-encoded paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The original safety check that normalized paths must start with the intended [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Behavior when decoding fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., fallback to the original, already-checked [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Fix in `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Always** URL-decode the entry name first [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalling back to the raw name on [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode errors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Then** resolve [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, normalize, and perform a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle prefix check against `parentPath`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Return the safe, normalized path if the check passes.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Steps to Implement  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocate the `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace its body with logic that:  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      i. Attempts to decode `[0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` into `decodedName`; on [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IllegalArgumentException` or `UnsupportedEncodingException`, uses the original [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ii. Forms `resolvedPath = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      iii. Throws an `IOException` if `![0m[1;35mresolvedPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      iv. Returns `resolvedPath`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove the old two-phase resolve [0m[35m/[0m[39m check [0m[35m/[0m[39m decode sequence to avoid bypass.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Rationale for Optimality  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach centralizes path traversal protection in the single `resolveIn` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod, ensuring every use of it [0m[1;39m([0m[39mall `Expander.expand` overloads[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m benefits.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Decoding before normalization and checking prevents decoded “..” segments from[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslipping past the safety check.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fallback behavior is preserved: decoding errors don’t cause failures but still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mget validated.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzzer harness, test code, or external dependencies—only the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable code path in the library itself.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entry names with special characters may be decoded to slightly different [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized paths, but they are immediately validated.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests that rely on the old two-step behavior should continue passing,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas legitimate entries will still map correctly.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a legitimate archive uses URL-encoded paths that resolve outside the target[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory, this stricter check will now reject them—which is desired to prevent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory traversal.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix aligns with standard “zip slip” protections found elsewhere in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., using `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` followed by `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the final [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prior Apache guidance on safe archive extraction recommends decoding first, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen normalization and prefix checks in a single, atomic step.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo additional file retrieval is necessary; the patch context is fully contained [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compile error “variable decodedName might already have been assigned” [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marises because `decodedName` is declared `final` and then assigned in both the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try` and `catch` blocks. Java’s definite‐assignment rules conflict with this [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranching assignment for a `final` local variable.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The deeper issue is that the existing `resolveIn` implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre‐patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplies URL decoding only after an initial traversal check on the raw entry name, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleaving URL‐encoded path‐traversal vectors unprotected. The correct approach is to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode first, then resolve+normalize, then check for traversal.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Steps[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocate the `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove the old two‐stage logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines that resolve and check the raw `name`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowed by a secondary decode‐and‐return[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, i.e.:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return outputFile;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Replace it with the following single, linear flow:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String decodedName;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If decoding fails, fall back to the raw entry name[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = name;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              parentPath, decodedName, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return outputFile;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Key changes:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Remove** the `final` modifier on `decodedName` to avoid double‐assignment[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconflicts.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Decode first** before any path resolution.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Normalize** only once on the decoded name.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Perform** the security check *after* normalization.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - **Return** the normalized, checked path.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We retain the method signature and overall behavior: generating a `Path` under[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is strengthening security by catching URL‐encoded traversal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code paths or API contracts are altered, so existing tests and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclients remain unaffected, except they now correctly reject malicious input.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side Effect**: Archive entries containing percent‐encoded characters now [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehave differently [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthey are decoded before resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. In rare cases where [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoding alters path structure even legitimately, applications that intentionally [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelied on raw percent‐encoded names will see a different resolution. [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     *Mitigation*: Document this change in the release notes as a security [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhardening, and it aligns with the principle of “least surprise” for percent‐encoded[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No broader utility changes**: Only the `resolveIn` default method is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This single‐pass decode→resolve→normalize→check pattern mirrors other [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure‐by‐default libraries that protect against “zip slip” vulnerabilities.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries or harness code are touched, in line with project [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguidelines.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn clean test` to ensure no test failures.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use a small reproducer archive with a URL‐encoded `..%2F` entry to confirm an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` is thrown.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that valid entries still extract correctly.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith these steps, the compilation error is resolved, and the security vulnerability[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mURL‐encoded path traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is fully mitigated. [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         An Apache Commons Compress fuzzer [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer`[1m)[0m triggered a critical           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path-traversal exception from Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer when expanding [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         an archive containing a name with “..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal.[0m” To mitigate, a patch    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was proposed in `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` that URL-decodes the entry name first,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         then normalizes and checks the resulting path. After applying the patch, the Maven  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         build fails with a Java compilation error in `ArchiveEntry.java`:                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “variable decodedName might already have been assigned.”                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Initial Issue                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A Jazzer fuzzing run hit                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         for path `[35m/tmp/[0m…[35m/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The sanitizer stack trace shows the violation originates from                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, invoked indirectly by `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         in multiple overloads, finally reached by `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates that an archive entry name containing “..[35m/[0m” sequences can lead to  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         extraction outside the target directory, triggering a detected security issue.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Patch Attempt                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Location:                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, method     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m`.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Original code:                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           final String name = [1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           final Path outputFile = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           if [1m([0m![1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               throw new [1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m;                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           try [1m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               return [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname, [33m...[0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1m}[0m catch [1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m [1m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m               return outputFile;                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Patched code:                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. Introduce `decodedName` and initialize it via `[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname,         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         US_ASCII[1m)[0m` inside a try-catch; on decode failure, fall back to `name`.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Compute `resolvedPath = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. If `![1;35mresolvedPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`, throw `[1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0mZip slip [33m...[0m[1m)[0m`.  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. `return resolvedPath`.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The diff removed the inner `try/catch` around resolving/decoding in the return    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and replaced it with a single decode + normalize + check block.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Patch-Resulting Build Log                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Maven compilation [1m([0m`mvn package`[1m)[0m recompiled [1;36m408[0m source files.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Compilation error in `ArchiveEntry.java` at line [1;36m84[0m:                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           variable decodedName might already have been assigned                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Areas for Further Investigation                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         after the patch; check if its presence affects variable flow analysis.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Normalization and Check Logic**                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Ensure the normalization and `startsWith` logic correctly protects against     [2m                [0m
